   |      |      |      |     |     |      |      |     |
   |:----:|-----:|:----:|:---:|:---:|:----:|:----:|:----|
   |      | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1679">+ y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1679">+y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1680">-y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1680">-y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1681">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1681">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1682">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1682">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1683">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1683">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1684">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1684">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1685">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1685">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1686">+x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1686">+x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1687">+ z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1687">+z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1688">~ z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1688">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1689">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1689">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1690">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1690">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1691">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1691">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1692">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1692">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1693">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1693">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1694">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1694">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1695">~ z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1695">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1696">+ z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1696">+z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1697">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1697">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1698">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1698">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1699">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1699">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1700">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1700">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1701">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1701">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1702">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1702">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1703">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1703">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1704">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1704">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1705">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1705">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1706">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1706">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1707">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1707">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1708">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1708">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1709">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1709">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1710">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1710">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1711">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1711">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1712">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1712">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1713">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1713">-0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1714">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1714">+0</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1715">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1715">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1716">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1716">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1717">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1717">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1718">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1718">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1719">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1719">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1720">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1720">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1721">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1721">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1722">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1722">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1723">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1723">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1724">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1724">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1725">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1725">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1726">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1726">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1727">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1727">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1728">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1728">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1729">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1729">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1730">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1730">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1731">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1731">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1732">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1732">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1733">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1733">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1734">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1734">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1735">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1735">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1736">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1736">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1737">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1737">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1738">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1738">NaN</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1739">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1739">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1740">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1740">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1741">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1741">NaN</span></span> | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1742">10 進数の乗算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1742">Decimal multiplication:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator *(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1743">結果の値が大きすぎてで表すかどうか、`decimal`形式、`System.OverflowException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1743">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1744">結果値はで表現するには小さすぎるかどうか、`decimal`形式、結果は 0 です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1744">If the result value is too small to represent in the `decimal` format, the result is zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1745">丸めを行う前に、結果の小数点以下桁数は、2 つのオペランドのスケールの合計です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1745">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the sum of the scales of the two operands.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1746">10 進数の乗算は型の乗算演算子を使用すると、`System.Decimal`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1746">Decimal multiplication is equivalent to using the multiplication operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="division-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1747">除算演算子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1747">Division operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1748">フォームの操作の`x / y`、二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決 ([二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) を適用して特定の演算子の実装を選択します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1748">For an operation of the form `x / y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1749">オペランドは、選択した演算子のパラメーターの型に変換され、結果の型が演算子の戻り値の型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1749">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1750">定義済みの除算演算子は、以下に示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1750">The predefined division operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1751">すべての演算子の商を計算する`x`と`y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1751">The operators all compute the quotient of `x` and `y`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1752">整数除算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1752">Integer division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator /(int x, int y);
   uint operator /(uint x, uint y);
   long operator /(long x, long y);
   ulong operator /(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1753">右側のオペランドの値が 0 の場合、`System.DivideByZeroException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1753">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1754">除算では、0 方向に結果を丸めます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1754">The division rounds the result towards zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1755">したがって、結果の絶対値が 2 つのオペランドの商の絶対値と等しいまたはそれより小さい最大整数です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1755">Thus the absolute value of the result is the largest possible integer that is less than or equal to the absolute value of the quotient of the two operands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1756">結果は、2 つのオペランドが同じ符号がある、または記号の反対側の 2 つのオペランドが負の場合は 0 または正の値。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1756">The result is zero or positive when the two operands have the same sign and zero or negative when the two operands have opposite signs.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1757">左側のオペランドが表現可能な最小の場合`int`または`long`値と右辺オペランドは`-1`オーバーフローが発生します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1757">If the left operand is the smallest representable `int` or `long` value and the right operand is `-1`, an overflow occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1758">`checked`コンテキスト、これにより、 `System.ArithmeticException` (またはそのサブクラス) がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1758">In a `checked` context, this causes a `System.ArithmeticException` (or a subclass thereof) to be thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1759">`unchecked`実装で定義されたかどうかは、そのコンテキストを`System.ArithmeticException`(またはそのサブクラス) がスローされますまたは結果の中、左側のオペランドの値に、オーバーフローが報告されません。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1759">In an `unchecked` context, it is implementation-defined as to whether a `System.ArithmeticException` (or a subclass thereof) is thrown or the overflow goes unreported with the resulting value being that of the left operand.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1760">浮動小数点除算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1760">Floating-point division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator /(float x, float y);
   double operator /(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1761">商は、IEEE 754 の演算の規則に従って計算されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1761">The quotient is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1762">次の表では、有限値が 0 以外の場合の可能なすべての組み合わせ、ゼロ、無限大および NaN の結果を示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1762">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1763">表に、`x`と`y`は正の有限値。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1763">In the table, `x` and `y` are positive finite values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1764">`z` 結果は、`x / y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1764">`z` is the result of `x / y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1765">変換先の型に対して、結果が大きすぎる場合`z`無限大です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1765">If the result is too large for the destination type, `z` is infinity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1766">変換先の型の結果が小さすぎる場合`z`は 0 です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1766">If the result is too small for the destination type, `z` is zero.</span></span>

   |      |      |      |      |      |      |      |      |
   |:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|

   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1790">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1790">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1791">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1791">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1792">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1792">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1793">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1793">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1794">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1794">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1795">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1795">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1796">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1796">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1797">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1797">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1798">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1798">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1799">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1799">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1800">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1800">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1801">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1801">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1802">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1802">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1803">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1803">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1804">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1804">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1805">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1805">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1806">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1806">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1807">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1807">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1808">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1808">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1809">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1809">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1810">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1810">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1811">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1811">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1812">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1812">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1813">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1813">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1814">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1814">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1815">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1815">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1816">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1816">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1817">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1817">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1818">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1818">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1819">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1819">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1820">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1820">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1821">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1821">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1822">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1822">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1823">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1823">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1824">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1824">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1825">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1825">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1826">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1826">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1827">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1827">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1828">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1828">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1829">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1829">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1830">小数除算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1830">Decimal division:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator /(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1831">右側のオペランドの値が 0 の場合、`System.DivideByZeroException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1831">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1832">結果の値が大きすぎてで表すかどうか、`decimal`形式、`System.OverflowException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1832">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1833">結果値はで表現するには小さすぎるかどうか、`decimal`形式、結果は 0 です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1833">If the result value is too small to represent in the `decimal` format, the result is zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1834">結果の小数点以下桁数と等しい、結果を保持する最小のスケール、実際の計算結果を 10 進値を表現できる最も近い。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1834">The scale of the result is the smallest scale that will preserve a result equal to the nearest representable decimal value to the true mathematical result.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1835">10 進数の除算は型の除算演算子を使用すると、`System.Decimal`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1835">Decimal division is equivalent to using the division operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="remainder-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1836">剰余演算子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1836">Remainder operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1837">フォームの操作の`x % y`、二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決 ([二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) を適用して特定の演算子の実装を選択します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1837">For an operation of the form `x % y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1838">オペランドは、選択した演算子のパラメーターの型に変換され、結果の型が演算子の戻り値の型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1838">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1839">定義済みの剰余演算子は、以下に示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1839">The predefined remainder operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1840">すべての演算子の間での除算の剰余を計算`x`と`y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1840">The operators all compute the remainder of the division between `x` and `y`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1841">整数の剰余。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1841">Integer remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator %(int x, int y);
   uint operator %(uint x, uint y);
   long operator %(long x, long y);
   ulong operator %(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1842">結果`x % y`によって値が生成される`x - (x / y) * y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1842">The result of `x % y` is the value produced by `x - (x / y) * y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1843">場合`y`0 の場合は、`System.DivideByZeroException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1843">If `y` is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1844">左側のオペランドが最も場合`int`または`long`値と右辺オペランドは`-1`、`System.OverflowException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1844">If the left operand is the smallest `int` or `long` value and the right operand is `-1`, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1845">ない場合は`x % y`例外をスロー場所`x / y`は例外をスローできません。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1845">In no case does `x % y` throw an exception where `x / y` would not throw an exception.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1846">浮動小数点の剰余。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1846">Floating-point remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator %(float x, float y);
   double operator %(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1847">次の表では、有限値が 0 以外の場合の可能なすべての組み合わせ、ゼロ、無限大および NaN の結果を示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1847">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1848">表に、`x`と`y`は正の有限値。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1848">In the table, `x` and `y` are positive finite values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1849">`z` 結果は、`x % y`を計算して`x - n * y`ここで、`n`に等しいまたはそれより小さい最大整数を`x / y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1849">`z` is the result of `x % y` and is computed as `x - n * y`, where `n` is the largest possible integer that is less than or equal to `x / y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1850">残りの部分をコンピューティングするのには、このメソッドは整数オペランドで使用される類似していますが、IEEE 754 の定義とは異なります (これで`n`に最も近い整数は、 `x / y`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1850">This method of computing the remainder is analogous to that used for integer operands, but differs from the IEEE 754 definition (in which `n` is the integer closest to `x / y`).</span></span>

   |:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|

   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1866">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1866">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1867">~ z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1867">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1868">~ z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1868">-z</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1869">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1869">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1870">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1870">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1871">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1871">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1872">-x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1872">-x</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1873">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1873">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1874">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1874">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1875">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1875">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1876">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1876">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1877">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1877">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1878">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1878">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1879">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1879">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1880">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1880">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1881">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1881">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1882">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1882">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1883">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1883">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1884">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1884">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1885">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1885">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1886">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1886">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1887">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1887">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1888">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1888">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1889">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1889">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1890">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1890">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1891">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1891">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1892">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1892">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1893">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1893">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1894">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1894">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1895">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1895">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1896">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1896">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1897">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1897">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1898">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1898">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1899">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1899">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1900">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1900">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1901">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1901">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1902">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1902">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1903">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1903">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1904">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1904">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1905">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1905">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1906">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1906">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1907">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1907">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1908">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1908">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1909">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1909">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1910">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1910">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1911">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1911">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1912">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1912">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1913">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1913">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1914">10 進数の剰余。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1914">Decimal remainder:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator %(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1915">右側のオペランドの値が 0 の場合、`System.DivideByZeroException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1915">If the value of the right operand is zero, a `System.DivideByZeroException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1916">丸めを行う前に、結果の小数点以下桁数は 2 つのオペランドの規模の大きいと、結果の符号は、0 以外の場合はいるのと同じ`x`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1916">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the larger of the scales of the two operands, and the sign of the result, if non-zero, is the same as that of `x`.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1917">10 進数の残りの部分は型の剰余演算子を使用すると`System.Decimal`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1917">Decimal remainder is equivalent to using the remainder operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>


### <a name="addition-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1918">加算演算子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1918">Addition operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1919">フォームの操作の`x + y`、二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決 ([二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) を適用して特定の演算子の実装を選択します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1919">For an operation of the form `x + y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1920">オペランドは、選択した演算子のパラメーターの型に変換され、結果の型が演算子の戻り値の型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1920">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1921">定義済みの加算演算子は、以下に示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1921">The predefined addition operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1922">数値型と列挙型の場合は、定義済みの加算演算子は、2 つのオペランドの合計を計算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1922">For numeric and enumeration types, the predefined addition operators compute the sum of the two operands.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1923">1 つまたは両方のオペランドが文字列型、定義済みの加算演算子はオペランドの文字列表現を連結します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1923">When one or both operands are of type string, the predefined addition operators concatenate the string representation of the operands.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1924">整数の加算:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1924">Integer addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator +(int x, int y);
   uint operator +(uint x, uint y);
   long operator +(long x, long y);
   ulong operator +(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1925">`checked`コンテキスト、合計が、結果の型の範囲外の場合、`System.OverflowException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1925">In a `checked` context, if the sum is outside the range of the result type, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1926">`unchecked`コンテキスト、オーバーフローが報告されず、結果型の範囲外有意の上位ビットは破棄されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1926">In an `unchecked` context, overflows are not reported and any significant high-order bits outside the range of the result type are discarded.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1927">浮動小数点加算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1927">Floating-point addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator +(float x, float y);
   double operator +(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1928">合計は、IEEE 754 の演算の規則に従って計算されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1928">The sum is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1929">次の表では、有限値が 0 以外の場合の可能なすべての組み合わせ、ゼロ、無限大および NaN の結果を示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1929">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaN's.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1930">表に、`x`と`y`は 0 以外の値の有限値と`z`の結果は、`x + y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1930">In the table, `x` and `y` are nonzero finite values, and `z` is the result of `x + y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1931">場合`x`と`y`絶対値が同じ記号、方向が逆`z`は正の 0 になります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1931">If `x` and `y` have the same magnitude but opposite signs, `z` is positive zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1932">場合`x + y`が大きすぎて、変換先の型で表す`z`、無限大と同じ符号で`x + y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1932">If `x + y` is too large to represent in the destination type, `z` is an infinity with the same sign as `x + y`.</span></span>

   |      |      |      |      |      |      |      |
   |:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|:----:|
   |      | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1933">Y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1933">y</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1934">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1934">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1935">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1935">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1936">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1936">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1937">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1937">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1938">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1938">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1939">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1939">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1940">z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1940">z</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1941">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1941">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1942">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1942">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1943">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1943">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1944">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1944">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1945">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1945">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1946">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1946">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1947">Y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1947">y</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1948">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1948">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1949">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1949">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1950">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1950">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1951">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1951">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1952">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1952">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1953">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1953">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1954">Y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1954">y</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1955">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1955">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1956">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1956">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1957">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1957">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1958">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1958">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1959">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1959">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1960">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1960">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1961">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1961">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1962">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1962">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1963">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1963">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1964">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1964">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1965">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1965">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1966">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1966">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1967">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1967">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1968">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1968">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1969">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1969">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1970">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1970">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1971">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1971">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1972">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1972">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1973">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1973">NaN</span></span>  | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1974">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1974">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1975">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1975">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1976">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1976">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1977">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1977">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1978">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1978">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1979">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1979">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1980">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1980">NaN</span></span>  | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1981">10 進数の追加:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1981">Decimal addition:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator +(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1982">結果の値が大きすぎてで表すかどうか、`decimal`形式、`System.OverflowException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1982">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1983">丸めを行う前に、結果の小数点以下桁数は 2 つのオペランドのスケールのうち、大きい方です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1983">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the larger of the scales of the two operands.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1984">10 進数の加算は型の加算演算子を使用すると、`System.Decimal`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1984">Decimal addition is equivalent to using the addition operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1985">列挙型の加算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1985">Enumeration addition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1986">すべての列挙型を暗黙的に、次の定義済みの演算子、提供、`E`列挙型と`U`の基になる型は、 `E`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1986">Every enumeration type implicitly provides the following predefined operators, where `E` is the enum type, and `U` is the underlying type of `E`:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   E operator +(E x, U y);
   E operator +(U x, E y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1987">実行時にこれらの演算子が正確に評価されます`(E)((U)x + (U)y)`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1987">At run-time these operators are evaluated exactly as `(E)((U)x + (U)y)`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1988">文字列の連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1988">String concatenation:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   string operator +(string x, string y);
   string operator +(string x, object y);
   string operator +(object x, string y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1989">これらのオーバー ロードのバイナリの`+`演算子が文字列の連結を実行します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1989">These overloads of the binary `+` operator perform string concatenation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1990">文字列の連結のオペランドは場合`null`、空の文字列に置き換えられます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1990">If an operand of string concatenation is `null`, an empty string is substituted.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1991">仮想を呼び出すことによって、任意の文字列以外の引数を文字列形式に変換がそれ以外の場合、`ToString`型から継承されたメソッド`object`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1991">Otherwise, any non-string argument is converted to its string representation by invoking the virtual `ToString` method inherited from type `object`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1992">場合`ToString`返します`null`、空の文字列に置き換えられます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1992">If `ToString` returns `null`, an empty string is substituted.</span></span>

   ```csharp
   using System;
   
   class Test
   {
       static void Main() {
           string s = null;
           Console.WriteLine("s = >" + s + "<");        // displays s = ><
           int i = 1;
           Console.WriteLine("i = " + i);               // displays i = 1
           float f = 1.2300E+15F;
           Console.WriteLine("f = " + f);               // displays f = 1.23E+15
           decimal d = 2.900m;
           Console.WriteLine("d = " + d);               // displays d = 2.900
       }
   }
   ```

   文字列連結演算子の結果は、左オペランドと右辺オペランドの文字が続くの文字で構成される文字列です。 文字列連結演算子が返すことはありません、`null`値。 <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1995">A`System.OutOfMemoryException`結果の文字列を割り当てることができる十分なメモリがない場合にスローされる可能性があります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1995">A `System.OutOfMemoryException` may be thrown if there is not enough memory available to allocate the resulting string.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1996">デリゲートの組み合わせ。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1996">Delegate combination.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1997">すべてのデリゲート型が暗黙的に次の定義済みの演算子を提供します、`D`はデリゲート型です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1997">Every delegate type implicitly provides the following predefined operator, where `D` is the delegate type:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   D operator +(D x, D y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1998">バイナリ`+`演算子は、両方のオペランドがいくつかのデリゲート型の場合、デリゲートの組み合わせを実行`D`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1998">The binary `+` operator performs delegate combination when both operands are of some delegate type `D`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-1999">(この場合、オペランドに異なるデリゲート型では、バインド時のエラーが発生します。)最初のオペランドが場合`null`、操作の結果は、2 番目のオペランドの値 (である場合でも`null`)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-1999">(If the operands have different delegate types, a binding-time error occurs.) If the first operand is `null`, the result of the operation is the value of the second operand (even if that is also `null`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2000">それ以外の場合、2 番目のオペランドが場合`null`操作の結果は最初のオペランドの値。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2000">Otherwise, if the second operand is `null`, then the result of the operation is the value of the first operand.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2001">それ以外の場合、操作の結果は、新しいデリゲート インスタンスが、呼び出される、最初のオペランドを呼び出すし、2 番目のオペランドを呼び出します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2001">Otherwise, the result of the operation is a new delegate instance that, when invoked, invokes the first operand and then invokes the second operand.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2002">デリゲートの組み合わせの例については、次を参照してください。[減算演算子](expressions.md#subtraction-operator)と[デリゲート呼び出し](delegates.md#delegate-invocation)します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2002">For examples of delegate combination, see [Subtraction operator](expressions.md#subtraction-operator) and [Delegate invocation](delegates.md#delegate-invocation).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2003">`System.Delegate` 、デリゲート型ではない`operator` `+`用に定義されていません。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2003">Since `System.Delegate` is not a delegate type, `operator` `+` is not defined for it.</span></span>

### <a name="subtraction-operator"></a><span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2004">減算演算子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2004">Subtraction operator</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2005">フォームの操作の`x - y`、二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決 ([二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) を適用して特定の演算子の実装を選択します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2005">For an operation of the form `x - y`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2006">オペランドは、選択した演算子のパラメーターの型に変換され、結果の型が演算子の戻り値の型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2006">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2007">定義済みの減算演算子は、以下に示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2007">The predefined subtraction operators are listed below.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2008">すべての減算演算子`y`から`x`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2008">The operators all subtract `y` from `x`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2009">整数の減算:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2009">Integer subtraction:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator -(int x, int y);
   uint operator -(uint x, uint y);
   long operator -(long x, long y);
   ulong operator -(ulong x, ulong y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2010">`checked`コンテキスト、違いが結果の型の範囲外の場合、`System.OverflowException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2010">In a `checked` context, if the difference is outside the range of the result type, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2011">`unchecked`コンテキスト、オーバーフローが報告されず、結果型の範囲外有意の上位ビットは破棄されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2011">In an `unchecked` context, overflows are not reported and any significant high-order bits outside the range of the result type are discarded.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2012">浮動小数点の減算:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2012">Floating-point subtraction:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   float operator -(float x, float y);
   double operator -(double x, double y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2013">違いは、IEEE 754 の演算の規則に従って計算されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2013">The difference is computed according to the rules of IEEE 754 arithmetic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2014">次の表では、0 以外の値の有限値の可能なすべての組み合わせ、ゼロ、無限大および Nan の結果を示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2014">The following table lists the results of all possible combinations of nonzero finite values, zeros, infinities, and NaNs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2015">表に、`x`と`y`は 0 以外の値の有限値と`z`の結果は、`x - y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2015">In the table, `x` and `y` are nonzero finite values, and `z` is the result of `x - y`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2016">場合`x`と`y`が等しいか、`z`は正の 0 になります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2016">If `x` and `y` are equal, `z` is positive zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2017">場合`x - y`が大きすぎて、変換先の型で表す`z`、無限大と同じ符号で`x - y`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2017">If `x - y` is too large to represent in the destination type, `z` is an infinity with the same sign as `x - y`.</span></span>

   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2024">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2024">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2025">z</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2025">z</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2026">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2026">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2027">x</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2027">x</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2028">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2028">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2029">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2029">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2030">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2030">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2031">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2031">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2032">-y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2032">-y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2033">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2033">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2034">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2034">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2035">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2035">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2036">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2036">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2037">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2037">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2038">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2038">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2039">-y</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2039">-y</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2040">-0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2040">-0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2041">+0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2041">+0</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2042">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2042">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2043">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2043">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2044">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2044">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2045">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2045">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2046">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2046">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2047">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2047">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2048">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2048">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2049">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2049">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2050">+inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2050">+inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2051">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2051">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2052">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2052">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2053">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2053">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2054">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2054">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2055">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2055">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2056">-inf</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2056">-inf</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2057">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2057">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2058">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2058">NaN</span></span> | 
   | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2059">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2059">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2060">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2060">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2061">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2061">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2062">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2062">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2063">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2063">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2064">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2064">NaN</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2065">NaN</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2065">NaN</span></span> | 

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2066">10 進数の減算:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2066">Decimal subtraction:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   decimal operator -(decimal x, decimal y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2067">結果の値が大きすぎてで表すかどうか、`decimal`形式、`System.OverflowException`がスローされます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2067">If the resulting value is too large to represent in the `decimal` format, a `System.OverflowException` is thrown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2068">丸めを行う前に、結果の小数点以下桁数は 2 つのオペランドのスケールのうち、大きい方です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2068">The scale of the result, before any rounding, is the larger of the scales of the two operands.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2069">10 進数の減算は、型の減算演算子を使用すると`System.Decimal`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2069">Decimal subtraction is equivalent to using the subtraction operator of type `System.Decimal`.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2070">列挙型の減算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2070">Enumeration subtraction.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2071">すべての列挙型が暗黙的に次の定義済みの演算子を提供、`E`列挙型と`U`の基になる型は、 `E`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2071">Every enumeration type implicitly provides the following predefined operator, where `E` is the enum type, and `U` is the underlying type of `E`:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   U operator -(E x, E y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2072">この演算子の評価とまったく同じ`(U)((U)x - (U)y)`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2072">This operator is evaluated exactly as `(U)((U)x - (U)y)`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2073">つまりの序数値の差の計算演算子`x`と`y`、列挙体の基になる型であり、結果の型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2073">In other words, the operator computes the difference between the ordinal values of `x` and `y`, and the type of the result is the underlying type of the enumeration.</span></span>

   ```csharp
   E operator -(E x, U y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2074">この演算子の評価とまったく同じ`(E)((U)x - y)`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2074">This operator is evaluated exactly as `(E)((U)x - y)`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2075">つまり、演算子は、減算、列挙体の基になる型の値列挙体の値として生成します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2075">In other words, the operator subtracts a value from the underlying type of the enumeration, yielding a value of the enumeration.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2076">デリゲートの削除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2076">Delegate removal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2077">すべてのデリゲート型が暗黙的に次の定義済みの演算子を提供します、`D`はデリゲート型です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2077">Every delegate type implicitly provides the following predefined operator, where `D` is the delegate type:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   D operator -(D x, D y);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2078">バイナリ`-`演算子は、両方のオペランドがいくつかのデリゲート型の場合、デリゲートの削除を実行`D`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2078">The binary `-` operator performs delegate removal when both operands are of some delegate type `D`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2079">オペランドに異なるデリゲート型がある場合、バインド時のエラーが発生します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2079">If the operands have different delegate types, a binding-time error occurs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2080">最初のオペランドが場合`null`、操作の結果は`null`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2080">If the first operand is `null`, the result of the operation is `null`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2081">それ以外の場合、2 番目のオペランドが場合`null`操作の結果は最初のオペランドの値。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2081">Otherwise, if the second operand is `null`, then the result of the operation is the value of the first operand.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2082">それ以外の場合、両方のオペランドが呼び出しリストを表す ([デリゲートの宣言](delegates.md#delegate-declarations)) 1 つまたは複数のエントリと、結果はから削除された、2 番目のオペランドのエントリで、最初のオペランドの一覧から成る新しい呼び出しリスト最初の連続するサブリストは、2 番目のオペランドの一覧を提供です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2082">Otherwise, both operands represent invocation lists ([Delegate declarations](delegates.md#delegate-declarations)) having one or more entries, and the result is a new invocation list consisting of the first operand's list with the second operand's entries removed from it, provided the second operand's list is a proper contiguous sublist of the first's.</span></span>     <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2083">(デリゲートの等値演算子とサブリスト、対応するエントリが比較されます ([デリゲート等値演算子](expressions.md#delegate-equality-operators)).)それ以外の場合、結果は、左側のオペランドの値です。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2083">(To determine sublist equality, corresponding entries are compared as for the delegate equality operator ([Delegate equality operators](expressions.md#delegate-equality-operators)).) Otherwise, the result is the value of the left operand.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2084">プロセスのどちらのオペランドのリストが変更されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2084">Neither of the operands' lists is changed in the process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2085">2 番目のオペランドの一覧には、最初のオペランドのリスト内の連続したエントリの複数のサブリストが一致すると、連続するエントリの右端の一致するサブリストは削除されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2085">If the second operand's list matches multiple sublists of contiguous entries in the first operand's list, the right-most matching sublist of contiguous entries is removed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2086">削除の結果、空のリストになる場合、結果は`null`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2086">If removal results in an empty list, the result is `null`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2087">例:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2087">For example:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   delegate void D(int x);
   
   class C
   {
       public static void M1(int i) { /* ... */ }
       public static void M2(int i) { /* ... */ }
   }

   class Test
   {
       static void Main() { 
           D cd1 = new D(C.M1);
           D cd2 = new D(C.M2);
           D cd3 = cd1 + cd2 + cd2 + cd1;   // M1 + M2 + M2 + M1
           cd3 -= cd1;                      // => M1 + M2 + M2
   
           cd3 = cd1 + cd2 + cd2 + cd1;     // M1 + M2 + M2 + M1
           cd3 -= cd1 + cd2;                // => M2 + M1
   
           cd3 = cd1 + cd2 + cd2 + cd1;     // M1 + M2 + M2 + M1
           cd3 -= cd2 + cd2;                // => M1 + M1
   
           cd3 = cd1 + cd2 + cd2 + cd1;     // M1 + M2 + M2 + M1
           cd3 -= cd2 + cd1;                // => M1 + M2
   
           cd3 = cd1 + cd2 + cd2 + cd1;     // M1 + M2 + M2 + M1
           cd3 -= cd1 + cd1;                // => M1 + M2 + M2 + M1
       }
   }
   ```

## <a name="shift-operators"></a><span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2088">シフト演算子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2088">Shift operators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2089">`<<`と`>>`演算子を使用して、ビット シフト演算を実行します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2089">The `<<` and `>>` operators are used to perform bit shifting operations.</span></span>

```antlr
shift_expression
    : additive_expression
    | shift_expression '<<' additive_expression
    | shift_expression right_shift additive_expression
    ;
```

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2090">オペランドの場合、 *shift_expression*コンパイル時の型を持つ`dynamic`、式を動的にバインドし、([動的バインド](expressions.md#dynamic-binding))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2090">If an operand of a *shift_expression* has the compile-time type `dynamic`, then the expression is dynamically bound ([Dynamic binding](expressions.md#dynamic-binding)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2091">この場合、式のコンパイル時の型は`dynamic`、コンパイル時の型を持つこれらのオペランドの実行時の型を使用して実行時に以下に示す解決が行わ`dynamic`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2091">In this case the compile-time type of the expression is `dynamic`, and the resolution described below will take place at run-time using the run-time type of those operands that have the compile-time type `dynamic`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2092">フォームの操作の`x << count`または`x >> count`、二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決 ([二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) を適用して特定の演算子の実装を選択します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2092">For an operation of the form `x << count` or `x >> count`, binary operator overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2093">オペランドは、選択した演算子のパラメーターの型に変換され、結果の型が演算子の戻り値の型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2093">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2094">最初のオペランドの型では、クラスまたは構造体の演算子の宣言を含むをある必要が常にオーバー ロードされた shift 演算子を宣言するときにあり、2 番目のオペランドの型は常にあります`int`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2094">When declaring an overloaded shift operator, the type of the first operand must always be the class or struct containing the operator declaration, and the type of the second operand must always be `int`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2095">定義済みのシフト演算子は、以下に示します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2095">The predefined shift operators are listed below.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2096">左にシフトします。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2096">Shift left:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator <<(int x, int count);
   uint operator <<(uint x, int count);
   long operator <<(long x, int count);
   ulong operator <<(ulong x, int count);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2097">`<<`演算子シフト`x`ビット数だけ左が以下に示すように計算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2097">The `<<` operator shifts `x` left by a number of bits computed as described below.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2098">結果型の範囲外の上位ビット`x`が破棄されるので、残りのビットが左にシフトされ、下位の空のビット位置が 0 に設定します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2098">The high-order bits outside the range of the result type of `x` are discarded, the remaining bits are shifted left, and the low-order empty bit positions are set to zero.</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2099">右シフトします。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2099">Shift right:</span></span>

   ```csharp
   int operator >>(int x, int count);
   uint operator >>(uint x, int count);
   long operator >>(long x, int count);
   ulong operator >>(ulong x, int count);
   ```

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2100">`>>`演算子シフト`x`ビット数だけ右が以下に示すように計算します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2100">The `>>` operator shifts `x` right by a number of bits computed as described below.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2101">ときに`x`の種類は`int`または`long`の下位ビット`x`は破棄されるので、残りのビットが右にシフトし、空の上位ビット位置は場合は 0 に設定されます`x`負でないと設定は、1 つの場合に`x`が負の値。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2101">When `x` is of type `int` or `long`, the low-order bits of `x` are discarded, the remaining bits are shifted right, and the high-order empty bit positions are set to zero if `x` is non-negative and set to one if `x` is negative.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2102">ときに`x`の種類は`uint`または`ulong`の下位ビット`x`が破棄されるので、残りのビットは右にシフトして、空の上位ビット位置が 0 に設定します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2102">When `x` is of type `uint` or `ulong`, the low-order bits of `x` are discarded, the remaining bits are shifted right, and the high-order empty bit positions are set to zero.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2103">定義済みの演算子のとおりにシフトするビット数が計算されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2103">For the predefined operators, the number of bits to shift is computed as follows:</span></span>

*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2104">場合の種類`x`は`int`または`uint`の下位 5 ビットで、シフト数を指定`count`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2104">When the type of `x` is `int` or `uint`, the shift count is given by the low-order five bits of `count`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2105">つまり、シフト数がから計算された`count & 0x1F`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2105">In other words, the shift count is computed from `count & 0x1F`.</span></span>
*  <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2106">場合の種類`x`は`long`または`ulong`の下位 6 ビットで、シフト数を指定`count`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2106">When the type of `x` is `long` or `ulong`, the shift count is given by the low-order six bits of `count`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2107">つまり、シフト数がから計算された`count & 0x3F`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2107">In other words, the shift count is computed from `count & 0x3F`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2108">シフト演算子は単の値を返す結果として得られる、シフト数が 0 の場合は、`x`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2108">If the resulting shift count is zero, the shift operators simply return the value of `x`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2109">オーバーフローが発生してで同じ結果を生成しないのシフト演算を`checked`と`unchecked`コンテキスト。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2109">Shift operations never cause overflows and produce the same results in `checked` and `unchecked` contexts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2110">ときの左オペランド、`>>`演算子が符号付き整数型は、算術右シフトのオペランドの最上位ビット (符号ビット) の値を反映する、空の上位ビット位置を実行します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2110">When the left operand of the `>>` operator is of a signed integral type, the operator performs an arithmetic shift right wherein the value of the most significant bit (the sign bit) of the operand is propagated to the high-order empty bit positions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2111">ときの左オペランド、`>>`演算子が符号なし整数型は、演算子、論理右シフトが行われ、空の上位ビット位置には常に 0 が設定されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2111">When the left operand of the `>>` operator is of an unsigned integral type, the operator performs a logical shift right wherein high-order empty bit positions are always set to zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2112">オペランドの型から推論の反対側の操作を実行するには、明示的なキャストを使用していることができます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2112">To perform the opposite operation of that inferred from the operand type, explicit casts can be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2113">たとえば場合、`x`型の変数は、 `int`、操作`unchecked((int)((uint)x >> y))`論理の右シフトを実行します。`x`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2113">For example, if `x` is a variable of type `int`, the operation `unchecked((int)((uint)x >> y))` performs a logical shift right of `x`.</span></span>

## <a name="relational-and-type-testing-operators"></a><span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2114">関係演算子と型検査演算子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2114">Relational and type-testing operators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2115">`==`、 `!=`、 `<`、 `>`、 `<=`、 `>=`、`is`と`as`演算子は、リレーショナルと型検査演算子と呼ばれます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2115">The `==`, `!=`, `<`, `>`, `<=`, `>=`, `is` and `as` operators are called the relational and type-testing operators.</span></span>

```antlr
relational_expression
    : shift_expression
    | relational_expression '<' shift_expression
    | relational_expression '>' shift_expression
    | relational_expression '<=' shift_expression
    | relational_expression '>=' shift_expression
    | relational_expression 'is' type
    | relational_expression 'as' type
    ;

equality_expression
    : relational_expression
    | equality_expression '==' relational_expression
    | equality_expression '!=' relational_expression
    ;
```

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2116">`is`演算子については、「 [、演算子は、](expressions.md#the-is-operator)と`as`演算子については、「[演算子として](expressions.md#the-as-operator)します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2116">The `is` operator is described in [The is operator](expressions.md#the-is-operator) and the `as` operator is described in [The as operator](expressions.md#the-as-operator).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2117">`==`、 `!=`、 `<`、 `>`、`<=`と`>=`演算子は***比較演算子***します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2117">The `==`, `!=`, `<`, `>`, `<=` and `>=` operators are ***comparison operators***.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2118">比較演算子のオペランドがコンパイル時の型を持つかどうか`dynamic`、式を動的にバインドし、([動的バインド](expressions.md#dynamic-binding))。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2118">If an operand of a comparison operator has the compile-time type `dynamic`, then the expression is dynamically bound ([Dynamic binding](expressions.md#dynamic-binding)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2119">この場合、式のコンパイル時の型は`dynamic`、コンパイル時の型を持つこれらのオペランドの実行時の型を使用して実行時に以下に示す解決が行わ`dynamic`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2119">In this case the compile-time type of the expression is `dynamic`, and the resolution described below will take place at run-time using the run-time type of those operands that have the compile-time type `dynamic`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2120">フォームの操作の`x` *op* `y`ここで、 *op*比較演算子をオーバー ロードの解決 ([二項演算子のオーバー ロードの解決](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) を適用して特定の演算子の実装を選択します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2120">For an operation of the form `x` *op* `y`, where *op* is a comparison operator, overload resolution ([Binary operator overload resolution](expressions.md#binary-operator-overload-resolution)) is applied to select a specific operator implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2121">オペランドは、選択した演算子のパラメーターの型に変換され、結果の型が演算子の戻り値の型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2121">The operands are converted to the parameter types of the selected operator, and the type of the result is the return type of the operator.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2122">定義済みの比較演算子は、次のセクションで説明します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2122">The predefined comparison operators are described in the following sections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2123">すべての定義済みの比較演算子は、型の結果を返す`bool`次の表で説明するようにします。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2123">All predefined comparison operators return a result of type `bool`, as described in the following table.</span></span>


| <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2124">__操作__</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2124">__Operation__</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2125">__結果__</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2125">__Result__</span></span>                                                       |
|---------------|------------------------------------------------------------------|
| `x == y`      | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2126">`true` 場合`x`と等しい`y`、`false`それ以外の場合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2126">`true` if `x` is equal to `y`, `false` otherwise</span></span>                 | 
| `x != y`      | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2127">`true` 場合`x`が等しくない`y`、`false`それ以外の場合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2127">`true` if `x` is not equal to `y`, `false` otherwise</span></span>             | 
| `x < y`       | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2128">`true` 場合`x`がより小さい`y`、`false`それ以外の場合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2128">`true` if `x` is less than `y`, `false` otherwise</span></span>                | 
| `x > y`       | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2129">`true` 場合`x`がより大きい`y`、`false`それ以外の場合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2129">`true` if `x` is greater than `y`, `false` otherwise</span></span>             | 
| `x <= y`      | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2130">`true` 場合`x`に等しいまたはそれよりも小さい`y`、`false`それ以外の場合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2130">`true` if `x` is less than or equal to `y`, `false` otherwise</span></span>    | 
| `x >= y`      | <span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2131">`true` 場合`x`がより大きいまたは等しい`y`、`false`それ以外の場合</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2131">`true` if `x` is greater than or equal to `y`, `false` otherwise</span></span> | 

### <a name="integer-comparison-operators"></a><span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2132">整数の比較演算子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2132">Integer comparison operators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2133">定義済みの整数の比較演算子は次のとおりです。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2133">The predefined integer comparison operators are:</span></span>
```csharp
bool operator ==(int x, int y);
bool operator ==(uint x, uint y);
bool operator ==(long x, long y);
bool operator ==(ulong x, ulong y);

bool operator !=(int x, int y);
bool operator !=(uint x, uint y);
bool operator !=(long x, long y);
bool operator !=(ulong x, ulong y);

bool operator <(int x, int y);
bool operator <(uint x, uint y);
bool operator <(long x, long y);
bool operator <(ulong x, ulong y);

bool operator >(int x, int y);
bool operator >(uint x, uint y);
bool operator >(long x, long y);
bool operator >(ulong x, ulong y);

bool operator <=(int x, int y);
bool operator <=(uint x, uint y);
bool operator <=(long x, long y);
bool operator <=(ulong x, ulong y);

bool operator >=(int x, int y);
bool operator >=(uint x, uint y);
bool operator >=(long x, long y);
bool operator >=(ulong x, ulong y);
```

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2134">返します、2 つの整数オペランドの数値を比較これらの各演算子を`bool`、特定の関係は、かどうかを示す値`true`または`false`します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2134">Each of these operators compares the numeric values of the two integer operands and returns a `bool` value that indicates whether the particular relation is `true` or `false`.</span></span>

### <a name="floating-point-comparison-operators"></a><span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2135">浮動小数点の比較演算子</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2135">Floating-point comparison operators</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2136">定義済みの浮動小数点数の比較演算子は次のとおりです。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2136">The predefined floating-point comparison operators are:</span></span>
```csharp
bool operator ==(float x, float y);
bool operator ==(double x, double y);

bool operator !=(float x, float y);
bool operator !=(double x, double y);

bool operator <(float x, float y);
bool operator <(double x, double y);

bool operator >(float x, float y);
bool operator >(double x, double y);

bool operator <=(float x, float y);
bool operator <=(double x, double y);

bool operator >=(float x, float y);
bool operator >=(double x, double y);
```

<span data-ttu-id="e26ba-2137">演算子は、IEEE 754 標準の規則に従ってオペランドを比較します。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="e26ba-2137">The operators compare the operands according to the rules of the IEEE 754 standard:</span></span>
